	$ebid.pdf.title = '개찰조서';
	$ebid.pdf.down('개찰조서_영동선 고사리-마차리간 118K320부근 방음벽 설치공사(변경공고).pdf');
}

function viewUnfitReason(reason) {

	// dialog
	$ebid.dialog.open({
		title: '부적격사유 조회',
		width: '400px'
	});
	
	//v IeProcConformJudgCS get-f20
}
